# Reanimated + React-Navigation 6 + RN 0.66.4

Reanimated 2.3.1 is supposed to work with chrome debug mode. Unfortunately if you're using @react-nativation/drawer then it just hangs on a black screen as soon as the app loads. This occurs on both iOS and Android.

This repo is a basic reproduction of the issue. Although it's caused by the drawer I think it's highly likely to be a reanimated issue as the drawer uses that extensively and there is some evidence that this is the cause on iOS\*.

Note that checking this on Android requires unreleased reanimated fixes (as of 10th Jan 2022) - I did this by downloading the latest build from Github actions and replacing the node_modules/react-native-reanimated with this build (as well as adding some pickFirsts to android/app/build.gradle to stop gradle failing).

I originally thought patch-package would actually handle this but it turns out not to handle binary files so the above does need to be done manually after cloning the repo to check Android.

\* Can't reproduce on this repo but on our production app we get an EXC_BAD_ACCESS crash with the following stack:
